# Awesome-Selfhosted

[![Awesome](_static/awesome.png)](https://github.com/sindresorhus/awesome) [![](https://github.com/awesome-selfhosted/awesome-selfhosted-data/actions/workflows/check-dead-links.yml/badge.svg)](https://github.com/awesome-selfhosted/awesome-selfhosted-data/issues/1) [![](https://github.com/awesome-selfhosted/awesome-selfhosted-data/actions/workflows/check-unmaintained-projects.yml/badge.svg)](https://github.com/awesome-selfhosted/awesome-selfhosted-data/issues/1) [![](https://img.shields.io/liberapay/goal/awesome-selfhosted?logo=liberapay)](https://liberapay.com/awesome-selfhosted/)

Self-hosting is the practice of hosting and managing applications on your own server(s) instead of consuming from üåé [SaaSS](www.gnu.org/philosophy/who-does-that-server-really-serve.html) providers.

This is a list of üåé [Free](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Free_software) Software üåé [network services](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Network_service) and üåé [web applications](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Web_application) which can be hosted on your own server(s). Non-Free software is listed on the [Non-Free](https://github.com/correia-jpv/fucking-awesome-selfhosted/blob/master/non-free.md) page.

* üåé [HTML version](awesome-selfhosted.net/) (recommended)**, [Markdown version](https://github.com/correia-jpv/fucking-awesome-selfhosted) (legacy).

See [Contributing](#contributing).

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**

_Related: [Content Management Systems (CMS)](#content-management-systems-cms)_

### Blogging Platforms

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**

A üåé [blog](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Blog) is a discussion or informational website consisting of discrete, diary-style text entries (posts).

_Related: [Static Site Generators](#static-site-generators), [Content Management Systems (CMS)](#content-management-systems-cms)_

_See also: üåé [WeblogMatrix](www.weblogmatrix.org/)_

### Calendar & Contacts

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**
 üåé [CalDAV](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/CalDAV) and üåé [CardDAV](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/CardDAV) protocol servers and web clients/interfaces for üåé [Electronic calendar](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Calendaring_software), üåé [address book](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Address_book) and üåé [contact management](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Contact_manager).

_Related: [Groupware](#groupware)_

_See also: üåé [Comparison of CalDAV and CardDAV implementations - Wikipedia](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Comparison_of_CalDAV_and_CardDAV_implementations)_

- üåé [Ba√Økal](sabre.io/baikal/) - Lightweight CalDAV and CardDAV server based on sabre/dav. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2926‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;300üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/sabre-io/Baikal))) `GPL-3.0` `PHP`
- üåé [DAViCal](www.davical.org/) - Server for calendar sharing (CalDAV) that uses a PostgreSQL database as a data store.  üåé [Source Code](gitlab.com/davical-project/davical)) `GPL-2.0` `PHP/deb`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;552‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;29üç¥</code></b> [Davis](https://github.com/tchapi/davis)) - A simple, dockerizable and fully translatable admin interface for sabre/dav based on Symfony 5 and Bootstrap 4, largely inspired by Ba√Økal. `MIT` `PHP`
- üåé [Manage My Damn Life](intri.in/manage-my-damn-life/) - Manage my Damn Life (MMDL) is a self-hosted front end for managing your CalDAV tasks and calendars. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;453‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;28üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/intri-in/manage-my-damn-life-nextjs))) `GPL-3.0` `Nodejs/Docker`

### Communication - Email - Mail Transfer Agents

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**
 üåé [Mail Transfer Agents](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Message_transfer_agent) (MTAs) - üåé [SMTP](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Simple_Mail_Transfer_Protocol) servers.

- üåé [chasquid](blitiri.com.ar/p/chasquid/) - SMTP (email) server with a focus on simplicity, security, and ease of operation.  üåé [Source Code](blitiri.com.ar/git/r/chasquid/)) `Apache-2.0` `Go`
- üåé [Courier MTA](www.courier-mta.org/) - Fast, scalable, enterprise mail/groupware server providing ESMTP, IMAP, POP3, webmail, mailing list, basic web-based calendaring and scheduling services.  üåé [Source Code](www.courier-mta.org/repo.html)) `GPL-3.0` `C/deb`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;251‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;53üç¥</code></b> [DragonFly](https://github.com/corecode/dma)) - A small MTA for home and office use. Works on Linux and FreeBSD. `BSD-3-Clause` `C`
- üåé [EmailRelay](emailrelay.sourceforge.net/) - A small and easy to configure SMTP and POP3 server for Windows and Linux.  üåé [Source Code](sourceforge.net/p/emailrelay/code/HEAD/tree/)) `GPL-3.0` `C++`
- üåé [Exim](www.exim.org/) - Message transfer agent (MTA) developed at the University of Cambridge.  üåé [Source Code](git.exim.org/exim.git)) `GPL-3.0` `C/deb`
- üåé [Haraka](haraka.github.io/) - Fast, highly extensible, and event driven SMTP server. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;5420‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;686üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/haraka/Haraka))) `MIT` `Nodejs`
- üåé [OpenSMTPD](opensmtpd.org/) - Secure SMTP server implementation from the OpenBSD project.  üåé [Source Code](cvsweb.openbsd.org/cgi-bin/cvsweb/src/usr.sbin/smtpd/)) `ISC` `C/deb`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;739‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;66üç¥</code></b> [OpenTrashmail](https://github.com/HaschekSolutions/opentrashmail)) - Complete trashmail solution that exposes an SMTP server and has a web interface to manage received emails. Works with multiple and wildcard domains and is fully file based (no database needed). Includes RSS feeds and JSON API. `Apache-2.0` `Python/PHP/Docker`
- [Postfix](http://www.postfix.org/) - Fast, easy to administer, and secure Sendmail replacement. `IPL-1.0` `C/deb`
- üåé [Sendmail](www.proofpoint.com/us/products/email-protection/open-source-email-solution) - Message transfer agent (MTA). `Sendmail` `C/deb`

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**
 üåé [Mailing list](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mailing_list) servers and mass mailing software - one message to many recipients.

- üåé [HyperKitty](wiki.list.org/HyperKitty) - Access GNU Mailman v3 archives.  üåé [Demo](lists.mailman3.org/), üåé [Source Code](gitlab.com/mailman/hyperkitty)) `GPL-3.0` `Python`
- üåé [Keila](www.keila.io) - Reliable and easy-to-use newsletter tool (alternative to Mailchimp and Sendinblue).  üåé [Demo](app.keila.io), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1855‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;122üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/pentacent/keila))) `AGPL-3.0` `Docker`
- üåé [Listmonk](listmonk.app/) - High performance, self-hosted newsletter and mailing list manager with a modern dashboard.  üåé [Demo](demo.listmonk.app/), <b><code>&nbsp;18104‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1796üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/knadh/listmonk))) `AGPL-3.0` `Go/Docker`
- üåé [Mailman](www.list.org/) - Manage electronic mail discussion and e-newsletter lists.  üåé [Source Code](gitlab.com/mailman/)) `GPL-3.0` `Python`
- üåé [Mautic](www.mautic.org/) - Marketing automation software (email, social and more). (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;8828‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;3059üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/mautic/mautic))) `GPL-3.0` `PHP`
- üåé [phpList](www.phplist.org) - Newsletter and email marketing with advanced management of subscribers, bounces, and plugins. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;821‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;273üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/phpList/phplist3))) `AGPL-3.0` `PHP`
- üåé [Postorius](docs.mailman3.org/projects/postorius/en/latest/) - Web user interface to access GNU Mailman.  üåé [Source Code](gitlab.com/mailman/postorius/)) `GPL-3.0` `Python`
- üåé [Schleuder](schleuder.nadir.org/) - GPG-enabled mailing list manager with resending-capabilities.  üåé [Source Code](0xacab.org/schleuder/schleuder/tree/master)) `GPL-3.0` `Ruby`
- üåé [Sympa](www.sympa.community/) - Mailing list manager. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;278‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;114üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/sympa-community/sympa))) `GPL-2.0` `Perl`

### Communication - SIP

(<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;169‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;73üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/BelledonneCommunications/flexisip))) `AGPL-3.0` `C/Docker`

- üåé [Routr](routr.io) - Lightweight SIP proxy, location server, and registrar for a reliable and scalable SIP infrastructure. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1603‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;169üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/fonoster/routr))) `MIT` `Docker/K8S`

- üåé [Wazo](wazo-platform.org/) - Full-featured IPBX solution built atop Asterisk with integrated Web administration interface and REST-ful API. ([Source Code](https://github.com/wazo-platform)) `GPL-3.0` `Python`

 üåé [DNS](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Domain_Name_System) servers and management tools with advertisement blocking functionality, primarily aimed at home or small networks.

_See also: <b><code>&nbsp;31570‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1848üç¥</code></b> [awesome-sysadmin/DNS - Servers](https://github.com/awesome-foss/awesome-sysadmin#dns---servers)), <b><code>&nbsp;31570‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1848üç¥</code></b> [awesome-sysadmin/DNS - Control Panels & Domain Management](https://github.com/awesome-foss/awesome-sysadmin#dns---control-panels--domain-management))_

- üåé [AdGuard Home](adguard.com/en/adguard-home/overview.html) - User-friendly ads & trackers blocking DNS server. (<b><code>&nbsp;30714‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2152üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/AdguardTeam/AdGuardHome))) `GPL-3.0` `Docker`

- üåé [Pi-hole](pi-hole.net/) - Blackhole for Internet advertisements with a GUI for management and monitoring. (<b><code>&nbsp;54020‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2899üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/pi-hole/pi-hole))) `EUPL-1.2` `Shell/PHP/Docker`
- üåé [Technitium DNS Server](technitium.com/dns/) - Authoritative/recursive DNS server with ad blocking functionality. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;6484‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;556üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/TechnitiumSoftware/DnsServer))) `GPL-3.0` `Docker/C#`


### Document Management

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**

A üåé [document management system](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Document_management_system) (DMS) is a system used to receive, track, manage and store documents and reduce paper.

- üåé [Docspell](docspell.org) - Auto-tagging document organizer and archive. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1938‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;151üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/eikek/docspell))) `GPL-3.0` `Scala/Java/Docker`

- üåé [Docuseal](www.docuseal.co) - Create, fill, and sign digital documents (alternative to DocuSign).  üåé [Demo](demo.docuseal.tech/), <b><code>&nbsp;10823‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;856üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/docusealco/docuseal))) `AGPL-3.0` `Docker`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;298‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;19üç¥</code></b> [EveryDocs](https://github.com/jonashellmann/everydocs-core)) - Simple Document Management System for private use with basic functionality to organize your documents digitally. `GPL-3.0` `Docker/Ruby`
- üåé [Gotenberg](gotenberg.dev) - Developer-friendly API to interact with powerful tools like Chromium and LibreOffice for converting numerous document formats (HTML, Markdown, Word, Excel, etc.) into PDF files, and more. (<b><code>&nbsp;10318‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;696üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/gotenberg/gotenberg))) `MIT` `Docker`

It provides a lot of extra features for students and research groups both in industry and academia.  üåé [Demo](i-librarian.net/demo/), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;311‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;32üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/mkucej/i-librarian-free))) `GPL-3.0` `PHP`
- üåé [Mayan EDMS](www.mayan-edms.com) - Electronic document management system for your documents with preview generation, OCR, and automatic categorization among other features.  üåé [Source Code](gitlab.com/mayan-edms/mayan-edms)) `GPL-2.0` `Docker/K8S`

- üåé [Paperless-ngx](docs.paperless-ngx.com/) - Scan, index, and archive all of your paper documents with an improved interface (fork of Paperless).  üåé [Demo](demo.paperless-ngx.com/), <b><code>&nbsp;33961‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2117üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/paperless-ngx/paperless-ngx))) `GPL-3.0` `Python/Docker`
- üåé [Papermerge](papermerge.com) - Document management system focused on scanned documents (electronic archives). Features file browsing in similar way to dropbox/google drive. OCR, full text search, text overlay/selection. - üåé [Papra](papra.app) - Minimalist document storage, management and archiving platform designed to be simple to use and accessible to everyone.  üåé [Demo](demo.papra.app/), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;?‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;?üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/papra-hq/papra/))) `AGPL-3.0` `Docker`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1355‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;64üç¥</code></b> [PdfDing](https://github.com/mrmn2/PdfDing)) - PDF manager, viewer and editor offering a seamless user experience on multiple devices. ### Document Management - E-books

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**

- üåé [Atsumeru](atsumeru.xyz) - Manga/comic/light novel media server with clients for Windows, Linux, macOS and Android. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;146‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/Atsumeru-xyz/Atsumeru)), üåé [Clients](atsumeru.xyz/guides/#how-does-it-work)) `MIT` `Java/Docker`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;424‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8üç¥</code></b> [BookLogr](https://github.com/Mozzo1000/booklogr)) - Manage your personal book library with ease.  üåé [Demo](demo.booklogr.app/)) `Apache-2.0` `Docker`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;5533‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;292üç¥</code></b> [BookLore](https://github.com/booklore-app/booklore)) - Host and manage books, with support for PDFs, eBooks, reading progress, metadata, and stats. `GPL-3.0` `Docker`
- <b><code>&nbsp;15803‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1658üç¥</code></b> [Calibre Web](https://github.com/janeczku/calibre-web)) - Browse, read and download eBooks using an existing Calibre database. `GPL-3.0` `Python`

- üåé [Kapowarr](casvt.github.io/Kapowarr/) - Build and manage a comic book library. Download, rename, move and convert issues of the volume to your liking. - üåé [kiwix-serve](www.kiwix.org/en/downloads/kiwix-serve/) - HTTP daemon for serving wikis from ZIM files. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;691‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;116üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/kiwix/kiwix-tools))) `GPL-3.0` `C++`

- [DSpace](http://www.dspace.org/) - Turnkey repository application providing durable access to digital resources. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1020‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1386üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/DSpace/DSpace))) `BSD-3-Clause` `Java`

- üåé [Fedora Commons Repository](wiki.lyrasis.org/display/FF/Fedora+Repository+Home) - Robust and modular repository system for the management and dissemination of digital content especially suited for digital libraries and archives, both for access and preservation. ### Document Management - Integrated Library Systems (ILS)

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**

An üåé [integrated library system](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Integrated_library_system) is an enterprise resource planning system for a library, used to track items owned, orders made, bills paid, and patrons who have borrowed.

_Related: [Content Management Systems (CMS)](#content-management-systems-cms), [Archiving and Digital Preservation (DP)](#archiving-and-digital-preservation-dp)_

- üåé [Evergreen](evergreen-ils.org) - Highly-scalable software for libraries that helps library patrons find library materials, and helps libraries manage, catalog, and circulate those materials. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;142‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;105üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/evergreen-library-system/Evergreen))) `GPL-2.0` `PLpgSQL`
- üåé [Koha](koha-community.org/) - Enterprise-class ILS with modules for acquisitions, circulation, cataloging, label printing, offline circulation for when Internet access is not available, and much more.  üåé [Demo](koha-community.org/demo/), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;537‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;272üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/Koha-Community/Koha))) `GPL-3.0` `Perl`
- üåé [RERO ILS](rero21.ch/) - Large-scale ILS that can be run as a service with consortial features, intended primarily for library networks. Includes most standard modules (circulation, acquisitions, cataloging,...) and a web-based public and professional interface.  üåé [Demo](ils.test.rero.ch/), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;81‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;29üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/rero/rero-ils))) `AGPL-3.0` `Python/Docker`

### Feed Readers

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**

A üåé [news aggregator](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/News_aggregator), also termed a feed aggregator, feed reader, news reader, üåé [RSS](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/RSS) reader, is an application that aggregates web content such as newspapers/blogs/vlogs/podcasts in one location for easy viewing.

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;219‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;55üç¥</code></b> [Bubo Reader](https://github.com/georgemandis/bubo-rss)) - Irrationally minimal RSS feed reader.  üåé [Demo](bubo-rss-demo.netlify.app/)) `MIT` `Nodejs`
- üåé [CommaFeed](www.commafeed.com/) - Google Reader inspired self-hosted RSS reader.  üåé [Demo](www.commafeed.com/#/app/category/all), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;3242‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;397üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/Athou/commafeed))) `Apache-2.0` `Java/Docker`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;254‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;23üç¥</code></b> [FeedCord](https://github.com/Qolors/FeedCord)) `‚ö†` - Simple, lightweight & customizable RSS News Feed for your Discord Server. `MIT` `Docker`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;383‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;27üç¥</code></b> [Feedpushr](https://github.com/ncarlier/feedpushr)) - Powerful RSS aggregator, able to transform and send articles to many outputs. Single binary, extensible with plugins. `GPL-3.0` `Go/Docker`
- üåé [Feeds Fun](feeds.fun/) - News reader with tags, scoring, and AI. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;285‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;14üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/Tiendil/feeds.fun))) `BSD-3-Clause` `Python`
- üåé [FreshRSS](freshrss.org/) - Self-hostable RSS feed aggregator.  üåé [Demo](demo.freshrss.org/i/), <b><code>&nbsp;12926‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1036üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/FreshRSS/FreshRSS))) `AGPL-3.0` `PHP/Docker`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1844‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;63üç¥</code></b> [Fusion](https://github.com/0x2E/fusion)) - Lightweight RSS aggregator and reader. `MIT` `Go/Docker`
- üåé [JARR](1pxsolidblack.pl/jarr-en.html) - JARR (Just Another RSS Reader) is a web-based news aggregator and reader (fork of Newspipe).  üåé [Demo](www.jarr.info/), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;128‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;14üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/jaesivsm/JARR))) `AGPL-3.0` `Docker/Python`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;285‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;54üç¥</code></b> [Kriss Feed](https://github.com/tontof/kriss_feed)) - Simple and smart (or stupid) feed reader. `CC0-1.0` `PHP`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;227‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;42üç¥</code></b> [Leed](https://github.com/LeedRSS/Leed)) - Leed (for Light Feed) is a Free and minimalist RSS aggregator. `AGPL-3.0` `PHP`
- üåé [Miniflux](miniflux.app/) - Minimalist news reader. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;8292‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;805üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/miniflux/v2))) `Apache-2.0` `Go/deb/Docker`
- üåé [NewsBlur](www.newsblur.com/) - Personal news reader that brings people together to talk about the world. A new sound of an old instrument. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;7169‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1020üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/samuelclay/NewsBlur))) `MIT` `Python`
- üåé [Newspipe](git.sr.ht/~cedric/newspipe) - Web news reader.  üåé [Demo](www.newspipe.org/signup)) `AGPL-3.0` `Python`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;77‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [Precis](https://github.com/leozqin/precis)) - Extensibility-oriented RSS reader that can use LLMs (including local LLMs) to summarize RSS entries with built-in notification support. `MIT` `Python/Docker`

### File Transfer - Object Storage & File Servers

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**
 üåé [Object storage](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Object_storage) is a computer data storage that manages data as objects, as opposed to other storage architectures like file systems which manages data as a file hierarchy, and block storage which manages data as blocks within sectors and tracks.

- üåé [GarageHQ](garagehq.deuxfleurs.fr/) - Geo-distributed, S3‚Äëcompatible storage service that can fulfill many needs.  üåé [Source Code](git.deuxfleurs.fr/Deuxfleurs/garage)) `AGPL-3.0` `Docker/Rust`

- <b><code>&nbsp;27034‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2524üç¥</code></b> [SeaweedFS](https://github.com/seaweedfs/seaweedfs)) - SeaweedFS is an open source distributed file system supporting WebDAV, S3 API, FUSE mount, HDFS, etc, optimized for lots of small files, and easy to add capacity. `Apache-2.0` `Go`
- <b><code>&nbsp;11195‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;865üç¥</code></b> [SFTPGo](https://github.com/drakkan/sftpgo)) - Flexible, fully featured and highly configurable SFTP server with optional FTP/S and WebDAV support. `AGPL-3.0` `Go/deb/Docker`

### Generative Artificial Intelligence (GenAI)

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**
 üåé [Generative Artificial Intelligence (GenAI)](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Generative_artificial_intelligence) is a subset of üåé [artificial intelligence](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Artificial_intelligence) that uses generative models to produce text, images, videos, or other forms of data.

- üåé [Agenta](agenta.ai/) - LLMOps platform for prompt management, LLM evaluation, and observability. Build, evaluate, and monitor production-grade LLM applications with collaborative prompt engineering. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;3312‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;391üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/agenta-ai/agenta))) `MIT` `Docker`

- üåé [Khoj](khoj.dev/) - Your AI second brain. Get answers from the web or your docs. Build custom agents, schedule automations, do deep research. Turn any online or local LLM into your personal, autonomous AI.  üåé [Demo](app.khoj.dev/), <b><code>&nbsp;31438‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1853üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/khoj-ai/khoj))) `AGPL-3.0` `Python/Docker`
- üåé [Ollama](ollama.com/) - Get up and running with Llama 3.3, DeepSeek-R1, Phi-4, Gemma 3, and other large language models. (<b><code>155137‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;13513üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/ollama/ollama))) `MIT` `Docker/Python`

- <b><code>&nbsp;27064‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2804üç¥</code></b> [Perplexica](https://github.com/ItzCrazyKns/Perplexica)) - AI-powered search engine (alternative to Perplexity AI). `MIT` `Docker`

### Groupware

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**

Collaborative software or üåé [groupware](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Collaborative_software) is designed to help people working on a common task to attain their goals. Groupware often regroups multiple services such as file sharing, calendar/events management, address books... in a single, integrated application.

- üåé [Citadel](www.citadel.org/) - Groupware including email, calendar/scheduling, address books, forums, mailing lists, IM, wiki and blog engines, RSS aggregation and more.  üåé [Source Code](www.citadel.org/source.html)) `GPL-3.0` `C/Docker/Shell`
- üåé [Colanode](colanode.com) - Collaboration suite with real-time messaging, rich text pages, file management, and dynamic databases - built for offline work (alternative to Slack, Notion). (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;4059‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;215üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/colanode/colanode))) `Apache-2.0` `K8S/Docker`
- üåé [Cozy Cloud](cozy.io/) - Personal cloud where you can manage and sync your files, notes, contacts, passwords, and documents. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;?‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;?üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/cozy/)), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;13üç¥</code></b> [Clients](https://github.com/cozy/cozy-store))) `GPL-3.0` `Nodejs`
- üåé [Digipad](digipad.app/) - An online self-hosted application for creating collaborative digital notepads (Documentation in french).  üåé [Source Code](codeberg.org/ladigitale/digipad)) `AGPL-3.0` `Nodejs`

### Internet of Things (IoT)

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**
 üåé [Internet of Things](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internet_of_things) describes physical objects with sensors, processing ability, software, and other technologies that connect and exchange data with other devices over the Internet.

- üåé [Domoticz](www.domoticz.com/) - Home Automation System that lets you monitor and configure various devices like: Lights, Switches, various sensors/meters like Temperature, Rain, Wind, UV, Electra, Gas, Water and much more. - üåé [EMQX](www.emqx.io/) - Scalable MQTT broker. Connect 100M+ IoT devices in one single cluster, move and process real-time IoT data with 1M msg/s throughput at 1ms latency.  üåé [Demo](www.emqx.com/en/mqtt/public-mqtt5-broker), <b><code>&nbsp;15434‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2390üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/emqx/emqx))) `Apache-2.0` `Docker/Erlang`
- üåé [evcc](evcc.io/) - Extensible Electric Vehicle Charge Controller and home energy management system. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;5657‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1081üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/evcc-io/evcc))) `MIT` `deb/Docker/Go`
- üåé [FHEM](fhem.de/fhem.html) - Automate common tasks in the household like switching lamps and heating. It can also be used to log events like temperature or power consumption. ### Media Streaming

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**
 üåé [Streaming media](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Streaming_media) is multimedia that is delivered and consumed in a continuous manner from a source, with little or no intermediate storage in network elements.

**Please visit [Media streaming - Audio Streaming](#media-streaming---audio-streaming), [Media streaming - Multimedia Streaming](#media-streaming---multimedia-streaming), [Media streaming - Video Streaming](#media-streaming---video-streaming), [Media Management](#media-management)**

_See also: üåé [List of streaming media systems - Wikipedia](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_streaming_media_systems), üåé [Comparison of streaming media systems - Wikipedia](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Comparison_of_streaming_media_systems)_

### Password Managers

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**

A üåé [password manager](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Password_manager) allows users to store, generate, and manage their passwords for local applications and online services.

- üåé [AliasVault](www.aliasvault.net) - End-to-end encrypted password manager with a built-in email alias generator and server. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1553‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;45üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/lanedirt/AliasVault))) `MIT` `Docker`
- üåé [Bitwarden](bitwarden.com/) `‚ö†` - Password manager with a webapp, browser extension, and mobile app. (<b><code>&nbsp;17349‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1464üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/bitwarden/server))) `AGPL-3.0` `Docker/C#`
- üåé [Passbolt](www.passbolt.com/) - Collaborative password manager. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;5404‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;357üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/passbolt/passbolt_api))) `AGPL-3.0` `PHP/deb/K8S/Docker`
- üåé [PassIt](passit.io/) - Simple password manage with sharing features by group and user, but no administration interface.  üåé [Demo](app.passit.io/), üåé [Source Code](gitlab.com/passit)) `AGPL-3.0` `Docker/Django`
- üåé [Passky](passky.org) - Simple and modern password manager with website, browser extension, android and desktop application.  üåé [Demo](vault.passky.org), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;237‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;30üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/Rabbit-Company/Passky-Server))) `GPL-3.0` `PHP/Docker`
- üåé [Psono](psono.com/) - Password manager for companies.  üåé [Demo](www.psono.pw), üåé [Source Code](gitlab.com/esaqa/psono/psono-fileserver)) `Apache-2.0` `Python`
- üåé [Teampass](teampass.net/) - Password manager dedicated for managing passwords in a collaborative way. One symmetric key is used to encrypt all shared/team passwords and stored server side in a file and the database. works on any server Apache, MySQL and PHP. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1756‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;564üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/nilsteampassnet/TeamPass))) `GPL-3.0` `PHP`
- <b><code>&nbsp;50368‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2351üç¥</code></b> [Vaultwarden](https://github.com/dani-garcia/vaultwarden)) - Lightweight Bitwarden server API implementation written in Rust. `GPL-3.0` `Rust/Docker`


### Pastebins

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**

A üåé [pastebin](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pastebin) is a type of online content-hosting service used for sharing and storing code and text.

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;599‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;57üç¥</code></b> [bin](https://github.com/w4/bin)) - A paste bin that's actually minimalist. `WTFPL/0BSD` `Rust`

Intended for one to few users looking for a simple pastebin deployment.  üåé [Demo](paste.wylke.it)) `Apache-2.0` `Java`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1836‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;86üç¥</code></b> [ByteStash](https://github.com/jordan-dalby/ByteStash)) - Pastebin and file storage service with a simple web interface. Supports syntax highlighting, optional user authentication and public sharing. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1836‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;86üç¥</code></b> [Demo](https://github.com/jordan-dalby/ByteStash?tab=readme-ov-file#demo))) `GPL-3.0` `Docker`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;63‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [Chiyogami](https://github.com/rhee876527/chiyogami)) - Pastebin with API, client-side encryption, user accounts, syntax highlighting, markdown rendering, and more.  üåé [Demo](chiyogami.myaddr.dev/)) `BSD-3-Clause` `Docker`
- üåé [dpaste](dpaste.org/) - Simple pastebin with multiple text and code option, with short url result easy to remember. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;579‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;127üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/DarrenOfficial/dpaste))) `MIT` `Docker/Django`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;470‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;68üç¥</code></b> [FlashPaper](https://github.com/AndrewPaglusch/FlashPaper)) - One-time encrypted zero-knowledge password/secret sharing application focused on simplicity and security. No database or complicated set-up required.  üåé [Demo](flashpaper.io)) `MIT` `Docker/PHP`
- üåé [Hemmelig](hemmelig.app) - Share encrypted secrets cross organizations, or as private persons. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;942‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;79üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/HemmeligOrg/Hemmelig.app))) `MIT` `Docker/Nodejs`
- üåé [lesma](lesma.eu) - Simple paste app friendly with browser and command line.  üåé [Demo](lesma.eu), üåé [Source Code](gitlab.com/ogarcia/lesma)) `GPL-3.0` `Rust/Docker`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;367‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8üç¥</code></b> [Local Content Share](https://github.com/Tanq16/local-content-share)) - Store and share text snippets and files within your local network. `MIT` `Docker/Go`
- üåé [not-th.re](not-th.re) - Simple paste sharing platform, with client side encryption, featuring the monaco browser-based code editor.  üåé [Demo](not-th.re), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;11‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/not-three/main))) `AGPL-3.0` `Nodejs/Docker`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2775‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;141üç¥</code></b> [Opengist](https://github.com/thomiceli/opengist)) - Pastebin powered by Git.  üåé [Demo](demo.opengist.io)) `AGPL-3.0` `Docker/Go/Nodejs`
- üåé [paaster](paaster.io) - End-to-end encrypted pastebin built with the objective of simplicity. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;498‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;22üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/WardPearce/paaster))) `AGPL-3.0` `Docker`
- üåé [pacebin](git.crueter.xyz/crueter/pacebin) - Super-minimal pastebin and file upload service focusing on small executable size, portability, and ease of configuration.  üåé [Demo](paste.crueter.xyz)) `AGPL-3.0` `C`
- üåé [Password Pusher](pwpush.com) - Dead-simple application to securely communicate passwords (or text) over the web. Passwords automatically expire after a certain number of views and/or time has passed. ### Proxy

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**

A üåé [proxy](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proxy_server) is a server application that acts as an intermediary between a client requesting a resource and the server providing that resource. This section about forward (i.e. outgoing) proxies. For reverse proxies, see the Web Server section.

_Related: [Web Servers](#web-servers)_

- üåé [g3proxy](g3-project.readthedocs.io/projects/g3proxy/en/latest/) - Forward proxy server supporting proxy chaining, protocol inspection, MITM Interception, ICAP adaptation and transparent proxy. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;772‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;61üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/bytedance/g3/tree/master/g3proxy))) `Apache-2.0` `Rust/deb`
- üåé [imgproxy](imgproxy.net/) - Fast and secure standalone server for resizing and converting remote images. (<b><code>&nbsp;10039‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;702üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/imgproxy/imgproxy))) `MIT` `Go/Docker/K8S`
- üåé [iodine](code.kryo.se/iodine/) - IPv4 over DNS tunnel solution, enabling you to start up a socks5 proxy listener. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;7404‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;562üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/yarrick/iodine))) `ISC` `C/deb`
- üåé [Outline Server](getoutline.org/) - A proxy server that runs a Shadowsocks instance for each access key and a REST API to manage the access keys. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;6093‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;867üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/Jigsaw-Code/outline-server))) `Apache-2.0` `Docker/Nodejs`
- üåé [Privoxy](www.privoxy.org) - Non-caching web proxy with advanced filtering capabilities for enhancing privacy, modifying web page data and HTTP headers, controlling access, and removing ads and other obnoxious Internet junk. `GPL-2.0` `C/deb`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;4388‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;325üç¥</code></b> [sish](https://github.com/antoniomika/sish)) - HTTP(S)/WS(S)/TCP tunnels to localhost using only SSH (serveo/ngrok alternative). `MIT` `Go/Docker`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;130‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;22üç¥</code></b> [socks5-proxy-server](https://github.com/nskondratev/socks5-proxy-server)) - SOCKS5 proxy server with built-in authentication and Telegram-bot for user management and user statistics on data spent (handy when you pay per GB of data). It is dockerised and simple to install. `Apache-2.0` `Docker`
- [Squid](http://www.squid-cache.org/) - Caching proxy for the Web supporting HTTP, HTTPS, FTP, and more. It reduces bandwidth and improves response times by caching and reusing frequently-requested web pages.  üåé [Source Code](code.launchpad.net/squid)) `GPL-2.0` `C/deb`
- üåé [Tinyproxy](tinyproxy.github.io/) - Light-weight HTTP/HTTPS proxy daemon. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;5496‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;737üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/tinyproxy/tinyproxy))) `GPL-2.0` `C/deb`
- üåé [txtdot](tempoworks.github.io/documentation) - A HTTP proxy that parses only text, links and pictures from pages reducing internet bandwidth usage, removing ads and heavy scripts.  üåé [Demo](txt.dc09.ru), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;193‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/TempoWorks/txtdot))) `MIT` `Nodejs/Docker`

### Remote Access

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**
 üåé [Remote desktop](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Remote_desktop_software) and üåé [SSH](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Secure_Shell) servers and web interfaces for remote management of computer systems.

- üåé [Engity's Bifr√∂st](bifroest.engity.org/) - Highly customizable SSH server with several ways to authorize a user and options where and how to execute a user's session. ### Search Engines

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**

A [search engine](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Search_engine_(computing)) is an üåé [information retrieval system](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Information_retrieval) designed to help find information stored on a computer system. This includes üåé [Web search engines](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Web_search_engine).

- üåé [Aleph](aleph.occrp.org/) - Tool for indexing large amounts of both documents (PDF, Word, HTML) and structured (CSV, XLS, SQL) data for easy browsing and search. It is built with investigative reporting as a primary use case.  üåé [Demo](aleph.occrp.org/), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2261‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;321üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/alephdata/aleph))) `MIT` `Docker/K8S`
- üåé [Apache Solr](lucene.apache.org/solr/) - Enterprise search platform featuring full-text search, hit highlighting, faceted search, real-time indexing, dynamic clustering, and rich document (e.g., Word, PDF) handling. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1500‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;774üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/apache/solr))) `Apache-2.0` `Java/Docker/K8S`
- üåé [Fess](fess.codelibs.org/) - Powerful and easily deployable Enterprise Search Server.  üåé [Demo](search.n2sm.co.jp/), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1062‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;168üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/codelibs/fess))) `Apache-2.0` `Java/Docker`
- <b><code>&nbsp;21778‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2235üç¥</code></b> [Jina](https://github.com/jina-ai/serve)) - Cloud-native neural search framework for any kind of data. `Apache-2.0` `Python/Docker`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;?‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;?üç¥</code></b> [Manticore Search](https://github.com/manticoresoftware/manticoresearch/)) - Full-text search and data analytics, with fast response time for small, medium and big data (alternative to Elasticsearch). `GPL-3.0` `Docker/deb/C++/K8S`
- üåé [MeiliSearch](www.meilisearch.com) - Ultra relevant, instant and typo-tolerant full-text search API. (<b><code>&nbsp;54283‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2238üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/meilisearch/MeiliSearch))) `MIT` `Rust/Docker/deb`

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1158‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;69üç¥</code></b> [sist2](https://github.com/sist2app/sist2)) - Lightning-fast file system indexer and search tool. `GPL-3.0` `C/Docker`

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;960‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;110üç¥</code></b> [Websurfx](https://github.com/neon-mmd/websurfx)) `‚ö†` - Aggregate results from other search engines (metasearch engine) without ads while keeping privacy and security in mind. (<b><code>&nbsp;17636‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;763üç¥</code></b> [Demo](https://github.com/zinclabs/zinc#playground-server)), <b><code>&nbsp;17636‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;763üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/zincsearch/zincsearch))) `Apache-2.0` `Go/Docker/K8S`

### Software Development - API Management

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**
 üåé [API management](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/API_management) is the process of creating and publishing üåé [application programming interfaces (APIs)](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/API), enforcing their usage policies, controlling access, nurturing the subscriber community, collecting and analyzing usage statistics, and reporting on performance. 

- üåé [DreamFactory](www.dreamfactory.com/) - Turns any SQL/NoSQL/Structured data into Restful API. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1693‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;343üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/dreamfactorysoftware/dreamfactory))) `Apache-2.0` `PHP/Docker/K8S`

- üåé [Fusio](www.fusio-project.org/) - Open-source API management platform which helps to build and manage REST APIs.  üåé [Demo](fusio-project.org/demo), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2051‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;235üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/apioo/fusio))) `AGPL-3.0` `PHP/Docker`
- üåé [Graphweaver](graphweaver.com/) - Turn multiple data sources into a single GraphQL API. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;542‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;27üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/exogee-technology/graphweaver))) `MIT` `Nodejs`
- üåé [Hasura](hasura.io) - Fast, instant realtime GraphQL APIs on Postgres with fine grained access control, also trigger webhooks on database events. (<b><code>&nbsp;31781‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2841üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/hasura/graphql-engine))) `Apache-2.0` `Haskell/Docker/K8S`
- üåé [Hoppscotch Community Edition](hoppscotch.io) - Fast and beautiful API request builder. (<b><code>&nbsp;76681‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;5379üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/hoppscotch/hoppscotch))) `MIT` `Nodejs/Docker`
- üåé [Kong](konghq.com/kong/) - Microservice API Gateway and Platform. (<b><code>&nbsp;42085‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;5007üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/Kong/kong))) `Apache-2.0` `Lua/Docker/K8S/deb`
- üåé [Lura](luraproject.org/) - High-performance API Gateway. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;6668‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;579üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/luraproject/lura))) `Apache-2.0` `Go`
- üåé [Opik](www.comet.com/site/products/opik/) `‚ö†` - Evaluate, test, and ship LLM applications with a suite of observability tools to calibrate language model outputs across your dev and production lifecycle. (<b><code>&nbsp;15324‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1151üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/comet-ml/opik))) `Apache-2.0` `Docker/Python`

- üåé [Svix](svix.com) - Open-source webhooks as a service that makes it super easy for API providers to send webhooks. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2969‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;217üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/svix/svix-webhooks))) `MIT` `Docker/Rust`

- üåé [Cgit](git.zx2c4.com/cgit/about/) - Fast lightweight web interface for git repositories.  üåé [Source Code](git.zx2c4.com/cgit/tree/)) `GPL-2.0` `C`
- üåé [Forgejo](forgejo.org) - A lightweight software forge focused on scaling, federation, and privacy (fork of Gitea).  üåé [Demo](next.forgejo.org), üåé [Source Code](codeberg.org/forgejo/forgejo/), üåé [Clients](codeberg.org/forgejo-contrib/delightful-forgejo)) `MIT` `Docker/Go`
- üåé [Fossil](www.fossil-scm.org/index.html/doc/trunk/www/index.wiki) - Distributed version control system featuring wiki and bug tracker. `BSD-2-Clause-FreeBSD` `C`

- üåé [gitbucket](gitbucket.github.io/) - Git platform powered with easy installation, high extensibility & GitHub API compatibility (alternative to GitHub). (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;9307‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1261üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/gitbucket/gitbucket))) `Apache-2.0` `Scala/Java`
- üåé [Gitea](gitea.com) - Git with a cup of tea! Painless self-hosted all-in-one software development service, including Git hosting, code review, team collaboration, package registry and CI/CD.  üåé [Demo](demo.gitea.com), <b><code>&nbsp;51741‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;6181üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/go-gitea/gitea))) `MIT` `Go/Docker/K8S`

### Status / Uptime pages

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**
 üåé [Uptime](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Uptime) is a measure of system reliability, expressed as the percentage of time a machine, typically a computer, has been working and available. 

_Related: [Monitoring](#monitoring)_

- üåé [cState](cstate.netlify.app/) - Static status page for hyperfast Hugo. Clean design, minimal JS, super light HTML/CSS, high customization, optional admin panel, read-only API, IE8+. Best used with Netlify, Docker.  üåé [Demo](cstate.mnts.lt/), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2773‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;249üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/cstate/cstate))) `MIT` `Go`
- üåé [Gatus](gatus.io/) - Automated service health dashboard.  üåé [Demo](status.twin.sh), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;8929‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;597üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/TwiN/gatus))) `Apache-2.0` `Docker/K8S`
- üåé [kener](kener.ing/) - Status page with incident management, easy to use and customize.  üåé [Demo](kener.ing/), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;4456‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;217üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/rajnandan1/kener))) `MIT` `Nodejs/Docker`
- üåé [Kuvasz Uptime](kuvasz-uptime.dev) - Performant, stable uptime & SSL monitoring service with brandable status pages, IAC support, Prometheus integration and a complete REST API.  üåé [Demo](kuvasz-uptime.dev/demo/), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;291‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;22üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/kuvasz-uptime/kuvasz))) `Apache-2.0` `Docker`
- üåé [StatPing.ng](statping-ng.github.io/) - An easy to use Status Page for your websites and applications. Statping will automatically fetch the application and render a beautiful status page with tons of features for you to build an even better status page. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1834‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;176üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/statping-ng/statping-ng))) `GPL-3.0` `Docker/Go`
- üåé [Uptime Kuma](uptime.kuma.pet/) - Self-hosted website monitoring tool like "Uptime Robot".  üåé [Demo](demo.kuma.pet), <b><code>&nbsp;77550‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;6859üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/louislam/uptime-kuma))) `MIT` `Docker/Nodejs`

### Ticketing

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**
 üåé [Helpdesk](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help_desk_software), üåé [bug](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bug_tracking_system) and üåé [issue](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Issue_tracking_system) tracking software to help the tracking of user requests, bugs and missing features.

_Related: [Task Management & To-do Lists](#task-management--to-do-lists), [Software Development - Project Management](#software-development---project-management)_

- üåé [Bugzilla](www.bugzilla.org/) - General-purpose bugtracker and testing tool originally developed and used by the Mozilla project. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;793‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;304üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/bugzilla/bugzilla))) `MPL-2.0` `Perl`
- üåé [Frappe Helpdesk](frappe.io/helpdesk) - Helpdesk software which helps you streamline your company's support, offers an easy setup, clean user interface, and automation tools to resolve customer queries efficiently. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2755‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;587üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/frappe/helpdesk))) `AGPL-3.0` `Docker`
- üåé [FreeScout](freescout.net/) - Email-based customer support application, help desk and shared mailbox (alternative to Zendesk and Help Scout).  üåé [Demo](demo.freescout.net/login), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;3855‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;604üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/freescout-help-desk/freescout))) `AGPL-3.0` `PHP/Docker`
- üåé [GlitchTip](glitchtip.com) - Error tracking app to collect errors reported by your app.  üåé [Source Code](gitlab.com/glitchtip/glitchtip)) `MIT` `Python/Docker/K8S`
- üåé [ITFlow](itflow.org) - Client IT documentation, ticketing, invoicing and accounting for MSPs (Managed Service Providers).  üåé [Demo](demo.itflow.org), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;824‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;214üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/itflow-org/itflow))) `GPL-3.0` `PHP`

### URL Shorteners

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**
 üåé [URL shortening](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/URL_shortening) is the action of shortening a üåé [URL](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Uniform_Resource_Locator) to make it substantially shorter and still direct to the required page. Before hosting one, please see üåé [disadvantages](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/URL_shortening#Disadvantages) of URL shorteners.

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;58‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [bit](https://github.com/sjdonado/bit)) - Fast, lightweight, resource-efficient, compiled URL shortener. `MIT` `Docker/Crystal`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;591‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;57üç¥</code></b> [Chhoto URL](https://github.com/SinTan1729/chhoto-url)) - Simple, lightning-fast URL shortener with no bloat (fork of simply-shorten). (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;591‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;57üç¥</code></b> [Demo](https://github.com/SinTan1729/chhoto-url?tab=readme-ov-file#demo)), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;591‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;57üç¥</code></b> [Clients](https://github.com/SinTan1729/chhoto-url/blob/main/TOOLS.md))) `MIT` `Rust/Docker`
- üåé [clink](git.crueter.xyz/crueter/clink) - A super-minimal link shortening service written in pure C, focusing on small executable size, portability, and ease of configuration.  üåé [Demo](short.crueter.xyz)) `AGPL-3.0` `C`
- üåé [Flink](gitlab.com/rtraceio/web/flink) - Create QR Codes, embeddable link previews for your website and crawls/scrapes metadata.  üåé [Demo](flink.is)) `MIT` `Docker`
- üåé [Kutt](kutt.it) - Modern URL shortener with support for custom domains and custom URLs.  üåé [Demo](kutt.it), <b><code>&nbsp;10225‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1380üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/thedevs-network/kutt))) `MIT` `Nodejs/Docker`
- üåé [rs-short](git.42l.fr/42l/rs-short) - Lightweight link shortener written in Rust, with features such as caching, spambot protection and phishing detection.  üåé [Demo](s.42l.fr/)) `MPL-2.0` `Rust`
- üåé [Shlink](shlink.io) - URL shortener with REST API and command line interface. Includes official progressive web application and docker images. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;4395‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;357üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/shlinkio/shlink)), üåé [Clients](shlink.io/apps)) `MIT` `PHP/Docker`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;57‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;17üç¥</code></b> [Simple-URL-Shortener](https://github.com/azlux/Simple-URL-Shortener)) - KISS URL shortener, public or private (with account). Minimalist and lightweight. No dependencies.  üåé [Demo](u.azlux.fr)) `MIT` `PHP`
- üåé [YOURLS](yourls.org/) - YOURLS is a set of PHP scripts that will allow you to run Your Own URL Shortener. Features include password protection, URL customization, bookmarklets, statistics, API, plugins, jsonp. (<b><code>&nbsp;11637‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2059üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/YOURLS/YOURLS))) `MIT` `PHP`

### VPN

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**

A üåé [virtual private network (VPN)](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_private_network) extends a private network across a public network and enables users to send and receive data across shared or public networks as if their computing devices were directly connected to the private network.

**Please visit <b><code>&nbsp;31570‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1848üç¥</code></b> [awesome-sysadmin/VPN](https://github.com/awesome-foss/awesome-sysadmin#vpn))**



### Web Servers

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**

Web Servers and Reverse Proxies. A üåé [web server](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Web_server) is a piece of software and underlying hardware that accepts requests via üåé [HTTP](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hypertext_Transfer_Protocol) (the network protocol created to distribute web content) or its secure variant üåé [HTTPS](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTTPS). A üåé [Reverse Proxy](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Reverse_proxy) is a proxy server that appears to any client to be an ordinary web server, but in reality merely acts as an intermediary that forwards requests to one or more ordinary web servers.

_Related: [Proxy](#proxy)_

- üåé [Algernon](algernon.roboticoverlords.org/) - Small self-contained pure-Go web server with Lua, Markdown, HTTP/2, QUIC, Redis and PostgreSQL support. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2952‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;146üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/xyproto/algernon))) `BSD-3-Clause` `Go/Docker`
- üåé [Apache HTTP Server](httpd.apache.org/) - Secure, efficient and extensible server that provides HTTP services in sync with the current HTTP standards.  üåé [Source Code](svn.apache.org/repos/asf/httpd/httpd/trunk/)) `Apache-2.0` `C/deb/Docker`
- üåé [BunkerWeb](www.bunkerweb.io) - Next-gen Web Application Firewall (WAF) that will protect your web services.  üåé [Demo](demo.bunkerweb.io), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;9306‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;529üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/bunkerity/bunkerweb)), üåé [Clients](docs.bunkerweb.io/latest/plugins/)) `AGPL-3.0` `deb/Docker/K8S/Python`
- üåé [Caddy](caddyserver.com/) - Powerful, enterprise-ready, open source web server with automatic HTTPS. (<b><code>&nbsp;67642‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;4521üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/caddyserver/caddy))) `Apache-2.0` `Go/deb/Docker`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2542‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;103üç¥</code></b> [go-doxy](https://github.com/yusing/godoxy)) - Lightweight, simple, and  performant reverse proxy with WebUI, Docker integration, automatic shutdown/startup for container based on traffic. `MIT` `Docker/Go`
- üåé [HAProxy](www.haproxy.org/) - Very fast and reliable reverse-proxy offering high availability, load balancing, and proxying for TCP and HTTP-based applications.  üåé [Source Code](git.haproxy.org/?p=haproxy.git;a=tree)) `GPL-2.0` `C/deb/Docker`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;147‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [Jauth](https://github.com/Jipok/Jauth)) `‚ö†` - Lightweight SSL/TLS reverse proxy with authorization (via Telegram and SSH) for self-hosted apps. `GPL-3.0` `Go`
- üåé [Lighttpd](www.lighttpd.net/) - Secure, fast, compliant, and very flexible web server that has been optimized for high-performance environments.  üåé [Source Code](git.lighttpd.net/lighttpd/lighttpd1.4)) `BSD-3-Clause` `C/deb/Docker`
- üåé [Nginx Proxy Manager](nginxproxymanager.com/) - Docker container for managing Nginx proxy hosts with a simple, powerful interface. (<b><code>&nbsp;29101‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;3350üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/NginxProxyManager/nginx-proxy-manager))) `MIT` `Docker`
- üåé [NGINX](nginx.org/en/) - HTTP and reverse proxy server, mail proxy server, and generic TCP/UDP proxy server. (<b><code>&nbsp;28389‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;7586üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/nginx/nginx))) `BSD-2-Clause` `C/deb/Docker`
- üåé [Pangolin](digpangolin.com/) - Identity-aware tunneled reverse proxy with dashboard UI, access control, and WireGuard-based tunnels (alternative to Cloudflare Tunnel, Tailscale). (<b><code>&nbsp;15855‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;465üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/fosrl/pangolin))) `AGPL-3.0` `Docker`
- üåé [Pomerium](www.pomerium.io) - Identity-aware reverse proxy, successor to now obsolete oauth_proxy. It inserts an OAuth step before proxying your request to the backend, so that you can safely expose your self-hosted websites to public Internet. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;4502‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;315üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/pomerium/pomerium))) `Apache-2.0` `Go/Docker`
- üåé [SafeLine](waf.chaitin.com/) - Web application firewall / reverse proxy to protect your web apps from attacks and exploits.  üåé [Demo](demo.waf.chaitin.com/), <b><code>&nbsp;18951‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1175üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/chaitin/SafeLine))) `GPL-3.0` `Docker`
- üåé [Static Web Server](static-web-server.net/) - Cross-platform, high-performance, and asynchronous web server for static file serving. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1989‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;109üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/static-web-server/static-web-server))) `Apache-2.0/MIT` `Rust/Docker`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;3473‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;274üç¥</code></b> [SWAG (Secure Web Application Gateway)](https://github.com/linuxserver/docker-swag)) - Nginx webserver and reverse proxy with PHP support, built-in Certbot (Let's Encrypt) client and fail2ban integration. `GPL-3.0` `Docker`
- üåé [Traefik](traefik.io/) - HTTP reverse proxy and load balancer that makes deploying microservices easy. (<b><code>&nbsp;57444‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;5542üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/traefik/traefik))) `MIT` `Go/Docker`
- üåé [UUSEC WAF](uuwaf.uusec.com) - Industry-leading high-performance, AI and semantic technology web application firewall and API security gateway (fork of nginx). (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1480‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;150üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/Safe3/uusec-waf))) `GPL-3.0` `C/Lua/Docker`
- üåé [Varnish](varnish-cache.org/) - Web application accelerator/caching HTTP reverse proxy. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;3990‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;398üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/varnishcache/varnish-cache))) `BSD-3-Clause` `Go/deb/Docker`
- üåé [Zoraxy](zoraxy.aroz.org/) - General purpose HTTP reverse proxy and forwarding tool. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;4487‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;254üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/tobychui/zoraxy))) `AGPL-3.0` `Go/Docker`


### Wikis

**[`^        back to top        ^`](#awesome-selfhosted)**

A üåé [wiki](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wiki) is a publication collaboratively edited and managed by its own audience directly using a web browser.

_Related: [Note-taking & Editors](#note-taking--editors), [Static Site Generators](#static-site-generators), [Knowledge Management Tools](#knowledge-management-tools)_

_See also: üåé [Wikimatrix](www.wikimatrix.org/), üåé [List of wiki software - Wikipedia](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_wiki_software), üåé [Comparison of wiki software - Wikipedia](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Comparison_of_wiki_software)_

- üåé [AmuseWiki](amusewiki.org/) - Amusewiki is based on the Emacs Muse markup, remaining mostly compatible with the original implementation. It can work as a read-only site, as a moderated wiki, or as a fully open wiki or even as a private site.  üåé [Demo](sandbox.amusewiki.org), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;204‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;27üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/melmothx/amusewiki))) `GPL-1.0` `Perl/Docker`
- üåé [BookStack](www.bookstackapp.com/) - Organize and store information. Stores documentation in a book like fashion.  üåé [Demo](www.bookstackapp.com/#demo), <b><code>&nbsp;17622‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2253üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/BookStackApp/BookStack))) `MIT` `PHP/Docker`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1897‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;585üç¥</code></b> [django-wiki](https://github.com/django-wiki/django-wiki)) - Wiki system with complex functionality for simple integration and a superb interface. Store your knowledge with style: Use django models.  üåé [Demo](demo.django-wiki.org/)) `GPL-3.0` `Python`
- üåé [docmost](docmost.com/) - Collaborative wiki and documentation software (alternative to Confluence, Notion). (<b><code>&nbsp;17716‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;983üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/docmost/docmost))) `AGPL-3.0` `Docker/Nodejs`
- üåé [Documize](documize.com) - Modern Docs + Wiki software with built-in workflow, single binary executable, just bring MySQL/Percona. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2330‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;235üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/documize/community))) `AGPL-3.0` `Go`
- üåé [Dokuwiki](www.dokuwiki.org/DokuWiki) - Easy to use, lightweight, standards-compliant wiki engine with a simple syntax allowing reading the data outside the wiki. All data is stored in plain text files, therefore no database is required. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;4451‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;900üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/dokuwiki/dokuwiki))) `GPL-2.0` `PHP`
- üåé [Feather Wiki](feather.wiki) - A lightning fast and infinitely extensible tool for creating personal non-linear notebooks, databases, and wikis that is entirely self-contained, runs in your browser, and is only 58 kilobytes in size.  üåé [Demo](feather.wiki/?page=gallery#wikis), üåé [Source Code](codeberg.org/Alamantus/FeatherWiki), üåé [Clients](feather.wiki/?page=gallery#extensions)) `AGPL-3.0` `Javascript`
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2245‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;228üç¥</code></b> [Gitit](https://github.com/jgm/gitit)) - Wiki program that stores pages and uploaded files in a git repository, which can then be modified using the VCS command line tools or the wiki's web interface. `GPL-2.0` `Haskell`
- <b><code>&nbsp;14169‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1564üç¥</code></b> [Gollum](https://github.com/gollum/gollum)) - Simple, Git-powered wiki with a sweet API and local frontend. `MIT` `Ruby`
- üåé [Mediawiki](www.mediawiki.org/wiki/MediaWiki) - Wiki software package that powers Wikipedia and all other Wikimedia projects, serving hundreds of millions of users each month.  üåé [Demo](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Main_Page), üåé [Source Code](phabricator.wikimedia.org/source/mediawiki/)) `GPL-2.0` `PHP`
- üåé [Mycorrhiza Wiki](mycorrhiza.wiki/) - Filesystem and git-based wiki engine written in Go using Mycomarkup as its primary markup language. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;?‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;?üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/bouncepaw/mycorrhiza/))) `AGPL-3.0` `Go`
- üåé [Oddmuse](oddmuse.org/) - Simple wiki engine written in Perl. No database required. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;86‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;14üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/kensanata/oddmuse))) `GPL-3.0` `Perl`
- üåé [Otter Wiki](otterwiki.com/) - Simple, easy to use wiki software using markdown. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1099‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;71üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/redimp/otterwiki))) `MIT` `Docker`
- üåé [PmWiki](www.pmwiki.org) - Wiki-based system for collaborative creation and maintenance of websites. `GPL-3.0` `PHP`
- üåé [Raneto](raneto.com/) - Knowledgebase platform that uses static Markdown files. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2848‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;442üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/ryanlelek/Raneto))) `MIT` `Nodejs`
- üåé [TiddlyWiki](tiddlywiki.com/) - Reusable non-linear personal web notebook. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;8443‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1239üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/TiddlyWiki/TiddlyWiki5))) `BSD-3-Clause` `Nodejs`
- üåé [Tiki](tiki.org/HomePage) - Wiki CMS Groupware with the most built-in features.  üåé [Demo](tiki.org/Try-Tiki), üåé [Source Code](gitlab.com/tikiwiki/tiki)) `LGPL-2.1` `PHP`
- üåé [W](w.club1.fr) - Lightweight, mutli-user, flat-file-database Wiki engine. Create pages quickly and edit them in your Web browser using Mardown/HTML/CSS/JS. The main difference with other wiki is that you are encouraged to customize each page style individually. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;44‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/vincent-peugnet/wcms))) `AGPL-3.0` `PHP`
- üåé [WackoWiki](wackowiki.org/) - WackoWiki is a light and easy to install multilingual Wiki-engine. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;54‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/WackoWiki/wackowiki))) `BSD-3-Clause` `PHP`
- üåé [Wiki-Go](leomoon.com/downloads/web-apps/wiki-go/) - A modern, feature-rich, databaseless flat-file wiki platform.  üåé [Demo](wikigo.leomoon.com), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;412‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;26üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/leomoon-studios/wiki-go))) `GPL-3.0` `Go/Docker`
- üåé [Wiki.js](js.wiki/) - Modern, lightweight and powerful wiki app using Git and Markdown.  üåé [Demo](docs.requarks.io), <b><code>&nbsp;27236‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;3085üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/Requarks/wiki))) `AGPL-3.0` `Nodejs/Docker/K8S`
- [WikiDocs](http://wikidocs.it) - A databaseless markdown flat-file wiki engine. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;449‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;53üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/Zavy86/WikiDocs))) `MIT` `PHP/Docker`
- üåé [WiKiss](wikiss.tuxfamily.org/) - Wiki, simple to use and install.  üåé [Source Code](svnweb.tuxfamily.org/listing.php?repname=wikiss/svn&path=%2F&sc=0)) `GPL-2.0` `PHP`
- üåé [XWiki](www.xwiki.org) - Second generation wiki that allows the user to extend its functionalities with a powerful extension-based architecture.  üåé [Demo](www.xwikiplayground.org/xwiki/bin/view/Main/), <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1149‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;602üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/xwiki/xwiki-platform))) `LGPL-2.1` `Java/Docker/deb`
- üåé [Zim](zim-wiki.org/) - Graphical text editor used to maintain a collection of wiki pages. Each page can contain links to other pages, simple formatting and images. (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2094‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;388üç¥</code></b> [Source Code](https://github.com/zim-desktop-wiki/zim-desktop-wiki))) `GPL-2.0` `Python/deb`
